<div class="margin-top-lg clearfix details-load-more details-more-placeholder">
<p class="word-wrap-break" id="ldp-detail-romance">Apartment #4A is on the building's southwest corner with stunning views of over Huntington Park and the front of Grace Cathedral. The apartment has recently been renovated including all new open kitchen, all new bathrooms, wood floors and recessed lighting. There is a private elevator entrance, high ceilings, wood burning fireplace, washer/dryer, and a balcony off the living room. The monthly assessment is $2, 632.00 which includes 24 hour doormen, use of fitness room, on site management and staff salaries, heat, water, reserve fund, ground lease, common area insurance and guest parking. THE NOB HILL, 1170 Sacramento Street, is a premier Nob Hill location and San Francisco's most sought after condominium address. Amenities include an elegantly landscaped drive in entrance with over a dozen guest parking spaces, a new fitness room, 24-hour doorman, security person for the service elevator, on site management, maintenance and janitorial personnel and valet guest parking.</p>

<div class="listing-subsection listing-subsection-features" id="ldp-detail-features">
<h3 class="header-subsection margin-bottom-lg">Property Features</h3>
<div>
<div class="load-more-features load-more-trigger" id="load-more-features">
<div class="row js-image-tag">
<div class="col-lg-3 col-sm-6 col-xs-6 col-xxs-12 ldp-features-image-tag with-image">

                  1170 Sacramento St Apt 4A, San Francisco, CA 94108 is a condo home for sale listed on the market for 3 days. 1170 Sacramento St Apt 4a is in the Nob Hill neighborhood, which has a median listing price of $1,588,000. The median listing price for Nob Hill is 14% greater than San Francisco at $1,399,000, and 189% greater than CA at $550,000. Nearby neighborhoods include <a href="https://www.realtor.com/realestateandhomes-search/Lower-Pacific-Heights_San-Francisco_CA/overview">Lower Pacific Heights</a>, <a href="https://www.realtor.com/realestateandhomes-search/Pacific-Heights_San-Francisco_CA/overview">Pacific Heights</a>, <a href="https://www.realtor.com/realestateandhomes-search/South-Beach_San-Francisco_CA/overview">South Beach</a> and <a href="https://www.realtor.com/realestateandhomes-search/Outer-Sunset_San-Francisco_CA/overview">Outer Sunset</a>.
